TCU was just coming off a 3 year probation and had no team to speak of.  Instead of playing 2nd-3rd string players Ware stayed in the entire game.  UofH had 6 wins and 2 losses in conference play, and they were on NCAA probation so they couldn't participate in a bowl game.  Yet, Ware still won the Davey O'Brien and the Heisman.  Go figure.
